Analysis** | Turn raw data into a coherent, time\u2011ordered, geo\u2011visualised story. | \u2022 Normalise all timestamps to UTC and to the device time zone. <br>\u2022 Build a chronological **timeline** of GPS fixes, Wi\u2011Fi scans, cellular events. <br>\u2022 Map the coordinates onto a GIS platform (ArcGIS, QGIS, Google Earth). <br>\u2022 Cross\u2011check with: <br>  \u2013 Known addresses (crime scene, suspect home). <br>  \u2013 Carrier CDR or SIM logs if obtainable. <br>  \u2013 Other evidence (CCTV, witness statements). | Turns disparate logs into a defensible narrative of the suspect's movements. |\n| **4. Reporting** | Deliver a clear, reproducible, and legally defensible account. | \u2022 Produce a **report** that follows NIST SP\u202f800\u2011101/800\u201186 structure: <br>  \u2013 Introduction & scope <br>  \u2013 Methodology (tools, commands, scripts) <br>  \u2013 Findings (tables, maps, timelines) <br>  \u2013 Conclusions <br>  \u2013 Appendices (check\u2011sums, logs). <br>\u2022 Include a **chain\u2011of\u2011custody** and **evidence integrity** section. | Gives the prosecution a document that can be examined in court, with all steps traceable. |\n\n---\n\n## 3.  Detailed Methodology\n\n### 3.1  Preparation & Planning\n\n| Task | Tool / Documentation | Justification |\n|------|----------------------|---------------|\n| Issue a valid **search warrant** and obtain **device\u2011forensic\u2011warrant** (FW) | \u2013 | Legal authority to collect and analyse the phone. |\n| Create a **Chain\u2011of\u2011Custody (CoC)** log (paper + electronic). | \u2013 | Ensures admissibility; every change of possession is recorded. |\n| Document **device metadata** (serial, IMEI, OS version, bootloader state, whether Knox is enabled). | \u2013 | Helps decide acquisition method and informs later analysis. |\n| Identify **external data sources** that may contain corroborating location info (Google account, Samsung Cloud, carrier). | \u2013 | Enables multi\u2011source validation. |\n| Assemble a **toolkit** and test each tool on a known\u2011good Samsung S23 image. | \u2013 | Avoids surprises in production. |\n\n#### Recommended Toolkit\n\n| Category | Tool | Why it fits the Samsung\u202fS23 |\n|----------|------|-----------------------------|\n| Physical acquisition | **Cellebrite Physical Analyzer** (PA) or **Oxygen Forensic Detective** (OFD) | Both support the latest Android phones and can extract data even from encrypted devices (via Knox or by using the device\u2019s own decryption key). |\n| Logical acquisition | **Cellebrite UFED** (Logical) | Simpler if the phone is unlocked and the investigator is short on time. |\n| Decryption | **Samsung Knox ToolKit** (forensic) | Extracts the device encryption keys from the secure element. |\n| Data parsing | **Oxygen Forensic Detective** (built\u2011in modules for Android, Google, Samsung Cloud, WhatsApp, etc.). <br> **Magnet AXIOM** | Offers a wide range of app parsers and timeline modules. |\n| File integrity | **FTK Imager**, **X\u2011Ways Forensics** | Compute MD5/SHA256 of the acquired image. |\n| Timeline & mapping | **Magnet AXIOM Timeline**, **Microsoft Excel**, **QGIS** (or ArcGIS), **Google Earth Pro** | Visualise and analyse location data. |\n| Logging & reproducibility | **Git**, **Jupyter Notebook** (Python) | Store scripts and commands for audit. |\n\n---\n\n### 3.2  Phase 1 \u2013 Collection\n\n| Step | Action | Tool | Notes |\n|------|--------|------|-------|\n| 1.1 | **Seal the device** in a tamper\u2011evident bag, label with case number and date. | \u2013 | Prevents accidental tampering during transport. |\n| 1.2 | **Obtain a physical image** using a forensic workstation (e.g., a dedicated forensic PC). | **Cellebrite PA** or **OFD** | Preferably use a **USB\u2011based write\u2011blocker** (e.g., for Android, a \u201cforensic\u201d USB\u2011to\u2011USB cable that passes the device in read\u2011only mode). |\n| 1.3 | **Verify image integrity**: compute MD5/SHA256 and record hashes. | **FTK Imager**, **X\u2011Ways** | Store hash values in the CoC. |\n| 1.4 | If the device is **locked** and not accessible, attempt to **unlock** using the suspect's credentials (if available) or by engaging **Samsung\u2019s Knox decryption**. | **Samsung Knox Toolkit**, **Cellebrite** | Legal constraints apply; only proceed with proper authorization. |\n| 1.5 | **Log all actions** (time, personnel, commands) in a secure log file. | \u2013 | Needed for the later \u201cexamination\u201d phase. |\n\n#### Justification\nA **physical image** preserves *all* data, including deleted files, in the exact state it was when seized.  The NIST 800\u201186 \u201cGuidelines for Digital Evidence\u201d recommends a physical acquisition for Android devices whenever possible because many forensic artifacts are stored in proprietary formats that may be lost with a logical fetch.\n\n---\n\n### 3.3  Phase 2 \u2013 Examination\n\n| Artifact | Extraction Method | Tool | Key Points |\n|----------|-------------------|------|------------|\n| **Android GPS logs** | `/sdcard/Android/data/com.google.android.location/` (or `/sdcard/Android/data/com.google.android.gms/`) | **Oxygen** or **Magnet** | The `location` database contains latitude/longitude, altitude, accuracy, and timestamp. |\n| **Google Location History** | `Google Takeout` (if the suspect\u2019s Google account is accessible) or `com.google.android.apps.location` backup | **OFD** (Google\u2011History parser) | Provides a more complete history (often 90\u2011days). |\n| **Samsung Cloud backup** | `Samsung Cloud` recovery (if enabled) | **Samsung Knox Toolkit** | May contain GPS data or \u201cMy Location\u201d history. |\n| **App logs** | \u2022 **WhatsApp**: `msgstore.db` <br>\u2022 **Telegram**: `td_lib` <br>\u2022 **Instagram**: `stories` <br>\u2022 **Snapchat**: `snapchat.db` <br>\u2022 **Google Maps**: `Maps` & `Google Timeline` | **OFD**, **Magnet** | Some apps record location when a post is made or a photo is taken. |\n| **System logs** | `logcat` dumps, `/data/system` | **OFD** | \u201cLocationProvider\u201d events show when the OS requested a location fix. |\n| **Wi\u2011Fi/Bluetooth** | `wlan` logs, `Bluetooth` logs | **OFD** | Each SSID/BSSID or BLE device ID can be mapped to a physical address (via Wi\u2011Fi\u2011DB or online BSSID databases). |\n| **Cellular tower** | `telephony` logs, `cellular_location.db` | **OFD** | Provides Cell ID, LAC, MCC/MNC. |\n| **Photos & media** | EXIF GPS tags | **ExifTool** | Some photos taken on the day may have GPS coordinates. |\n| **Bixby/Voice commands** | `Bixby` log files | **OFD** | \u201cShow me the nearest restaurant\u201d often logs the location. |\n| **Samsung Health / SmartThings** | `com.samsung.android.app.shealth` | **OFD** | May contain movement data (steps, runs). |\n\n#### Extraction Process\n\n1. **Load the image into the forensic suite.**  \n2. **Run the built\u2011in \u201cLocation\u201d module** (Oxygen or Magnet).  \n3. **Export raw data** (CSV, JSON).  \n4. **Export app\u2011specific databases** to a local directory for independent parsing.  \n5. **Save all exported files** with SHA256 checksums.  \n\n#### Validation / Quality Control\n\n- Compare timestamps across multiple sources to spot inconsistencies.  \n- Verify that the device\u2019s system clock is set to the correct time zone.  \n- Use **ExifTool** to confirm photo GPS tags match the extracted coordinates.  \n\n---\n\n### 3.4  Phase 3 \u2013 Analysis\n\n| Sub\u2011task | Tool | Output | Justification |\n|----------|------|---------|---------------|\n| **3.1 Normalise timestamps** | **Python** (`pytz`, `datetime`) | UTC\u2011converted timestamps | Eliminates confusion from time\u2011zone or daylight\u2011saving changes. |\n| **3.2 Build a timeline** | **Magnet AXIOM Timeline**, **Chrono** | Chronological list of events with coordinates | Provides a narrative of movement. |\n| **3.3 Map coordinates** | **QGIS** or **ArcGIS** (GeoJSON import) | Map overlay of suspect path | Visual proof of location. |\n| **3.4 Correlate with known addresses** | **Google Maps** or **OpenStreetMap** | Distance calculations between points and crime scene | Quantifies proximity. |\n| **3.5 Cross\u2011check with external sources** | **Carrier CDR** (if available), **Google Takeout** | Additional confirmation of location | Strengthens confidence. |\n| **3.6 Identify gaps** | **Data gaps** in the timeline | Flag periods where no GPS fix is available | Helps explain missing evidence. |\n| **3.7 Verify integrity** | **SHA256** of extracted files, **hash\u2011based checks** | Assurance that data has not been altered | Required for court admissibility. |\n\n#### Example Workflow\n\n1. **Import CSV** of GPS records into QGIS.  \n2. **Add a \u201cTime\u201d field** and enable the **\u201cTemporal\u201d** plugin.  \n3. **Play the timeline** to visualise the suspect\u2019s movement.  \n4. **Overlay crime scene coordinates** (obtained from the police).  \n5. **Export a PNG/\u200bPDF** of the trajectory for inclusion in the final report.  \n\n#### Handling Encryption / Decryption\n\n- If the device is **Knox\u2011encrypted**, use the **Samsung Knox Toolkit** to retrieve the **Master Key** from the secure element.  \n- Feed the key to **Cellebrite** or **OFD** to decrypt the file system.  \n- If decryption fails, note the limitation and consider obtaining the **Google account credentials** to download encrypted backups (e.g., Google Takeout).  \n\n---\n\n### 3.5  Phase 4 \u2013 Reporting\n\n### 4.1  Report Structure (NIST 800\u2011101 compliant)\n\n| Section | Content | Tool/Artifact |\n|---------|---------|---------------|\n| **1. Executive Summary** | Brief answer to the question. | \u2013 |\n| **2. Scope & Objectives** | What was examined, why. | \u2013 |\n| **3. Methodology** | Detailed description of each phase, tools used, commands. | Tool logs, scripts. |\n| **4. Evidence Handling** | Chain\u2011of\u2011Custody, integrity checks, storage details. | CoC log, hash values. |\n| **5. Findings** | \u2022 Table of GPS points (date, time, latitude, longitude, accuracy). <br>\u2022 Map images (trajectory, crime scene). <br>\u2022 Correlation tables (device time \u2194 UTC, Google History \u2194 device). | Exported CSVs, GIS maps, screenshots. |\n| **6. Analysis & Interpretation** | Narrative of suspect movement, distance calculations, gaps. | Timeline, GIS analysis. |\n| **7. Limitations** | Missing data, encryption, possible tampering. | \u2013 |\n| **8. Conclusion** | Final statement: \u201cThe suspect was at X location at Y time.\u201d | \u2013 |\n| **Appendix** | Tool configuration files, raw logs, hash values, source code. | \u2013 |\n\n### **4.2  Deliverables**\n\n| Deliverable | Format | Where to store |\n|--------------|--------|----------------|\n| **Forensic Image** | Encrypted, read\u2011only disk image (`.dd`, `.img`) | Secure evidence repository (e.g., EnCase Evidence File). |\n| **Extracted Data** | CSV/JSON | Forensic workspace, backed up to a read\u2011only copy. |\n| **Map Visualization** | PDF/PNG | Report appendix. |\n| **Chain\u2011of\u2011Custody** | PDF/Word | Evidence log, stored with the image. |\n| **Tool Logs & Scripts** | Text files, Git repository | For audit trail. |\n\n### **4.3  Legal & Quality Assurance**\n\n- **Chain\u2011of\u2011Custody**: Each person who handled the device signs the CoC.  \n- **Evidence Integrity**: All images and extracted files are hashed, and the hash values are included in the report.  \n- **Re\u2011examination**: A second examiner reviews the report and marks.  \n- **Documentation**: All tools, versions, and command\u2011line arguments are recorded.  \n\n---\n\n## 4.  Justification of the Approach\n\n| Phase | Why this method? | NIST Reference |\n|-------|------------------|----------------|\n| **Collection** | Physical acquisition preserves *all* information, including deleted files, which is vital when location logs can be overwritten. | NIST SP\u202f800\u201186, \u201cGuidelines for Digital Evidence\u201d. |\n| **Examination** | Using industry\u2011standard forensic suites guarantees that the extraction process is repeatable and that artifacts are parsed correctly. | NIST SP\u202f800\u2011101, \u201cDigital Forensics\u201d. |\n| **Analysis** | Normalising timestamps and mapping coordinates turns data into a story that can be understood by a judge or jury. | NIST SP\u202f800\u201186, \u201cChronology and Timeline Analysis\u201d. |\n| **Reporting** | A structured, auditable report satisfies the admissibility criteria in most courts (e.g., Daubert). | NIST SP\u202f800\u2011101, \u201cReporting Standards\u201d. |\n\n---\n\n## 5.  Practical Tips & Pitfalls\n\n| Issue | Mitigation |\n|-------|-------------|\n| **Device is locked** | Obtain the PIN/password from the suspect (if possible); otherwise use **Knox decryption**. |\n| **Location data missing** | Look for *indirect* evidence: photo EXIF, app logs, Wi\u2011Fi/Bluetooth. |\n| **Multiple time zones** | Always convert to UTC before analysis. |\n| **Encrypted backups** | Use the suspect\u2019s Google account to download a **Takeout** archive; it is not encrypted and contains Location History. |\n| **Carrier logs unavailable** | Seek a **Cellular CDR** request from the provider (often a court order is required). |\n| **Data gaps** | Note the gaps, but do not over\u2011interpret the absence of a GPS fix (e.g., indoor, no satellite). |\n| **Chain\u2011of\u2011Custody breach** | Re\u2011take the evidence, re\u2011image, and document the breach. |\n\n---\n\n## 6.  Sample Workflow (Command Line / Scripts)\n\n```bash\n# 1. Acquire image\ncpa -i /dev/usb0 -o s23_image.dd -r\n\n# 2. Verify integrity\nmd5sum s23_image.dd\nsha256sum s23_image.dd\n\n# 3. Load image into OFD\noifd -i s23_image.dd -o /tmp/ofer\n\n# 4. Extract location database\noifd -extract db /tmp/ofer/Android/data/com.google.android.location/database/location.db -o /tmp/loc\n\n# 5. Parse and normalise\npython normalise_timestamps.py /tmp/loc/location.csv -o /tmp/loc_norm.csv\n\n# 6. Import into QGIS\nqgis --project /tmp/loc_project.qgs --run /tmp/loc_norm.csv\n\n# 7. Export map\nqgis --project /tmp/loc_project.qgs --export /tmp/loc_map.pdf\n```\n\n*All scripts and tool configurations should be stored in a **Git** repository (branch per phase).*\n\n---\n\n## 7. The combination of raw GPS fixes, Google/Samsung Location History, app logs, and external corroboration (Wi\u2011Fi/Bluetooth, cellular) provides a robust, court\u2011admissible conclusion. Magnet).  \n3. **Export raw data** (CSV, JSON).  \n4. **Export app\u2011specific databases** to a local directory for independent parsing.  \n5. **Save all exported files** with SHA256 checksums. Justification of the Approach\n\n| Phase | Why this method? | NIST Reference |\n|-------|------------------|----------------|\n| **Collection** | Physical acquisition preserves *all* information, including deleted files, which is vital when location logs can be overwritten. | NIST SP\u202f800\u201186, \u201cGuidelines for Digital Evidence\u201d. |\n| **Examination** | Using industry\u2011standard forensic suites guarantees that the extraction process is repeatable and that artifacts are parsed correctly. | NIST SP\u202f800\u2011101, \u201cDigital Forensics\u201d. |\n| **Analysis** | Normalising timestamps and mapping coordinates turns data into a story that can be understood by a judge or jury. | NIST SP\u202f800\u201186, \u201cChronology and Timeline Analysis\u201d. |\n| **Reporting** | A structured, auditable report satisfies the admissibility criteria in most courts (e.g., Daubert). | NIST SP\u202f800\u2011101, \u201cReporting Standards\u201d. |\n\n---\n\n## 5.  Practical Tips & Pitfalls\n\n| Issue | Mitigation |\n|-------|-------------|\n| **Device is locked** | Obtain the PIN/password from the suspect (if possible); otherwise use **Knox decryption**. |\n| **Location data missing** | Look for *indirect* evidence: photo EXIF, app logs, Wi\u2011Fi/Bluetooth. |\n| **Multiple time zones** | Always convert to UTC before analysis. |\n| **Encrypted backups** | Use the suspect\u2019s Google account to download a **Takeout** archive; it is not encrypted and contains Location History. |\n| **Carrier logs unavailable** | Seek a **Cellular CDR** request from the provider (often a court order is required). |\n| **Data gaps** | Note the gaps, but do not over\u2011interpret the absence of a GPS fix (e.g., indoor, no satellite). |\n| **Chain\u2011of\u2011Custody breach** | Re\u2011take the evidence, re\u2011image, and document the breach. |\n\n---\n\n## 6.  Sample Workflow (Command Line / Scripts)\n\n```bash\n# 1. Acquire image\ncpa -i /dev/usb0 -o s23_image.dd -r\n\n# 2. Verify integrity\nmd5sum s23_image.dd\nsha256sum s23_image.dd\n\n# 3. Parse and normalise\npython normalise_timestamps.py /tmp/loc/location.csv -o /tmp/loc_norm.csv\n\n# 6. Import into QGIS\nqgis --project /tmp/loc_project.qgs --run /tmp/loc_norm.csv\n\n# 7. Export map\nqgis --project /tmp/loc_project.qgs --export /tmp/loc_map.pdf\n```\n\n*All scripts and tool configurations should be stored in a **Git** repository (branch per phase).*\n\n---\n\n## 7. Practical Considerations & Legal Safeguards\n\n| Issue | Recommendation |\n|-------|----------------|\n| **Device Encryption** | If the phone is encrypted and locked, attempt to obtain the pass\u2011phrase directly from the suspect (if possible); otherwise, rely on carrier/Google logs or a lawful request to Samsung to unlock the Knox container. |\n| **Legal Authority** | Secure a search warrant for the device. For carrier/log\u2011in data, obtain a subpoena or court order. Document all legal authorisations in the chain of custody. |\n| **Data Privacy** | Only collect data strictly necessary for the question (location on 15\u202fJan). Mask or redact unrelated personal data before sharing. |\n| **Volatile Data** | If the device is still powered on, consider a **live acquisition** (e.g., using ADB or a forensics tablet) to capture RAM\u2011based logs. Note that this may alter the device state, so document the process fully. |\n| **Multiple Log Sources** | Android stores location data in several places: `com.google.android.location`, `com.samsung.android.app.location`, `WifiLogs.db`, `CellInfo`, `AndroidProvider`. Ensure all are examined to avoid missing data. |\n| **Time\u2011zone & NTP** | Verify that the device\u2019s system clock was accurate on 15\u202fJan. If not, adjust timestamps before analysis. |\n| **Carrier Data Quality** | Carrier logs may have 5\u201110\u202fm resolution (cell\u2011tower) or 50\u202fm (Wi\u2011Fi). Document the precision in the report. |\n| **Device Wear & Battery** | Note if the device was turned off or had a low battery on the crime date, as this can explain missing GPS points. |\n\n---\n\n## 5. Justification of the NIST 4\u2011Phase Model\n\n| Phase | Alignment with NIST | Why it Fits |\n|-------|---------------------|-------------|\n| **Collection** | NIST SP\u202f800\u201186 recommends preservation of the original evidence and creation of a forensic image. | We collect a write\u2011protected image, document the device, and preserve all ancillary sources. |\n| **Examination** | NIST stresses thorough, documented data extraction and verification. | We use multiple extraction methods, hash\u2011verify, and document every artefact. |\n| **Analysis** | NIST requires correlation, interpretation, and verification of findings. | We build timelines, map locations, cross\u2011check with external data, and quantify uncertainty. |\n| **Reporting** | NIST mandates a clear, reproducible report with chain of custody and evidence overview. | We produce a structured report and attach all logs, maps, and chain\u2011of\u2011custody documentation. |\n\n---\n\n## 8. Introduction & Legal Context  \n\n| Item | Detail |\n|------|--------|\n| **Case objective** | Establish the *geographical position* of the suspect on **15\u202fJan\u202f2024** (the day of the homicide). |\n| **Device under scrutiny** | Samsung Galaxy\u202fS23 (Android\u00a014, 256\u202fGB, fully encrypted, Samsung\u202fKnox\u202fenabled). |\n| **Legal basis** | Forensic acquisition and examination performed under a valid search warrant / subpoena. All actions must respect the **U.S. Federal Rules of Evidence** (Rule\u00a0901), **NIST\u202f800\u201186** guidelines and the **APIS** (Acquisition, Processing, Analysis, and Reporting Standards). |\n| **NIST 4\u2011Phase Model** | 1) **Collection** \u2013 secure, seize, image. <br>2) **Examination** \u2013 verify integrity, inventory, file system mapping. <br>3) **Analysis** \u2013 data\u2011parsing, timeline construction, geolocation mapping. <br>4) **Reporting** \u2013 chain of custody, methodology, findings, conclusions. |\n\n> **Why NIST?**  \n> The four\u2011phase framework enforces a **structured, repeatable, defensible** process that allows the court to evaluate the validity of the evidence. Each step has built\u2011in auditability (hashes, logs, chain of custody) and aligns with the **Digital Evidence and Forensics (DEF) Toolkit** used by most U.S. agencies.\n\n---\n\n## 2.  Phase 1 \u2013 Collection\n\n| Step | What to Do | Why It Matters | Suggested Tools |\n|------|-------------|----------------|-----------------|\n| **2.1. Evidence Preparation** | \u2022 Document *device* (IMEI, serial, model). <br>\u2022 Photograph the device in situ (front, side, power button). <br>\u2022 Record *witness statements* (if any). | Establishes **context** and a baseline for later comparison. | Smartphone camera, field logbook, chain\u2011of\u2011custody sheet. |\n| **2.2. Physical Acquisition (Full Digital Image)** | \u2022 Power\u2011off the phone (if possible). <br>\u2022 Remove the **SD\u2011card** (if present). <br>\u2022 Connect to a **JTAG/EDL** adapter (Samsung\u00a0S23 uses *Fastboot* or *EDL*). <br>\u2022 Extract the **bootloader, system, userdata, cache** partitions. | Captures *all* data, including deleted files, hidden partitions, and protected storage (Knox, EFS). | \u2022 **Cellebrite Physical Analyzer** (supports Samsung\u00a0S23 / Knox). <br>\u2022 **Oxygen Forensics Physical Analyzer** (supports full\u2011partition image). <br>\u2022 **Magnet AXIOM** (EDL/FASTBOOT support). |\n| **2.3. Logical Acquisition (If Device Is Unlocked)** | \u2022 Enable **USB debugging**. <br>\u2022 Pull the *data* partition via **ADB** (`adb pull`). <br>\u2022 Pull *Google Play Services* databases, *Location Services* caches, *app data* (WhatsApp, Instagram, Telegram). | Provides a *quick* snapshot with minimal wear on the device. | **ADB**, **Cellebrite UFED** (logical mode), **Oxygen** (logical mode). |\n| **2.4. Cloud & Account\u2011Based Data** | \u2022 Request *Google Account* \u201cLocation History\u201d via **Google Takeout**. <br>\u2022 Request *Samsung Cloud* backups (via Samsung\u2019s \u201cFind My Mobile\u201d). | Some location data is stored on the cloud and may survive a factory reset or encryption of the local storage. | **Google Takeout**, **Samsung Cloud** interface. |\n| **2.5. Integrity Verification** | \u2022 Compute **SHA\u2011256** (and MD5) for every image / file created. <br>\u2022 Store hash values in a *tamper\u2011proof* log (e.g., immutable ledger, write\u2011once\u2011read\u2011many disk). | Ensures that the evidence has not been altered between acquisition and analysis. | **Hashdeep**, **FTK Imager**, **Aegis** (chain\u2011of\u2011custody). |\n| **2.6. Chain of Custody Documentation** | \u2022 Record *person* acquiring, *time*, *location*, *method*, *storage* conditions. <br>\u2022 Sign and store the chain\u2011of\u2011custody sheet in a *tamper\u2011evident* envelope. | Required by law to prove admissibility. | Chain\u2011of\u2011custody template, digital signature. |\n\n### Key Considerations for the S23\n\n| Issue | Mitigation |\n|-------|------------|\n| **Device encryption** (Android Keystore + Knox) | Use *Knox\u2011enabled* forensic tools that can read the **Knox EFS** and **Secure Boot** partitions. |\n| **Secure Boot & Verified Boot** | Verify that the bootloader signatures match Samsung\u2019s official keys; any mismatch indicates tampering. |\n| **Remote wipe** | Verify that the device was not remotely wiped (e.g., \u201cFind My Mobile\u201d \u2192 \u201cErase\u201d). |\n| **Battery state** | Record battery level; low battery may affect logging. |\n\n---\n\n## 3.  Phase 2 \u2013 Examination\n\nThe goal of Examination is to **inventory** the acquired data and locate *all sources* that can provide location information.\n\n| Step | Activity | Justification | Tools |\n|------|----------|---------------|-------|\n| **3.1. Verify Acquisition Integrity** | \u2022 Re\u2011hash each image/file. <br>\u2022 Compare with stored hashes. | Confirms that the acquisition was *intact* before any processing. | **Hashdeep**, **FTK Imager**. |\n| **3.2. File System Mapping** | \u2022 Mount the *userdata* ext4 image. <br>\u2022 Use *file system forensics* to list directories, timestamps. | Identifies where Android stores *location logs* and *app data*. | **Autopsy**, **FTK**, **Mount\u2011Windows / ext4**. |\n| **3.3. Identify Location\u2011Related Databases** | \u2022 Search for: `fused_location_provider`, `LocationManager`, `GooglePlayServices`, `com.google.android.gms.location`. <br>\u2022 Search for *SQLite* databases with location tables (`locations`, `history`). | The core of Android\u2019s location service is stored here. | **SQLite3**, **Autopsy SQLite plugin**, **Magnet AXIOM**. |\n| **3.4. Extract GPS Coordinates** | \u2022 Parse the `fused_location_provider` DB \u2192 `location` table (lat, lon, accuracy, provider, timestamp). <br>\u2022 Parse `Google Maps` cache (e.g., `maps.db`, `timeline.db`). | Provides *raw* latitude/longitude with timestamps. | **Custom Python/SQLite scripts** (pandas), **Oxygen**. |\n| **3.5. Extract Wi\u2011Fi & Cell Tower Records** | \u2022 Parse `/data/misc/wifi/wpa_supplicant.conf` and `/data/misc/wifi/wifi.log`. <br>\u2022 Extract BSSID/SSID, signal strength, timestamp. <br>\u2022 Parse `telephony` logs for `CellTower` IDs, LAC, CID, PSC. | Wi\u2011Fi BSSID and cell IDs can be *geo\u2011referenced* using public databases. | **Wireshark** (for log parsing), **OpenCellID** API, **Mozilla Location Service**. |\n| **3.6. Extract Samsung Knox logs** | \u2022 Pull `knox_efs` and `knox_log` directories. <br>\u2022 Look for `device_location` tables. | Knox may store *additional* location data in a protected partition. | **Knox SDK** (for forensic extraction), **Cellebrite**. |\n| **3.7. Extract Third\u2011Party App Geotags** | \u2022 Parse `WhatsApp/Media/WhatsApp\u00a0Images` for EXIF GPS. <br>\u2022 Parse `Telegram` media metadata. <br>\u2022 Parse `Instagram` caches for media geotags. | App data may contain *user\u2011generated* location evidence (e.g., photos, messages). | **ExifTool**, **Oxygen**, **FTK**. |\n| **3.8. Extract Logcat & System Logs** | \u2022 Pull `/data/misc/logcat/` and `logcat.log`. <br>\u2022 Search for `LocationManager`, `FusedLocationProvider`. | Logs often contain *timestamped* location updates even if the DB is deleted. | **Logcat Viewer**, **Autopsy**. |\n| **3.9. Extract Battery & Sensor Data** | \u2022 Pull `/data/system/batterystats.xml`. <br>\u2022 Look for *battery discharges* that coincide with location updates. | Helps confirm device activity at specific times. | **BatteryStats Analyzer**. |\n| **3.10. Cross\u2011Check Timestamps** | \u2022 Convert all timestamps to *UTC* and to the **local time zone** of the suspect (if known). | Avoids mis\u2011interpretation of location windows. | **Chrono**, **Python datetime**. |\n\n### Deliverables from Examination\n\n| Deliverable | Content |\n|--------------|---------|\n| **Device Inventory** | List of partitions, files, sizes, timestamps. |\n| **Extracted Location Tables** | CSV/Excel file with `datetime`, `lat`, `lon`, `accuracy`, `provider`. |\n| **Wi\u2011Fi & Cell Tower Logs** | BSSID/SSID, LAC/CID, timestamps. |\n| **Knox Log Summary** | Any location events. |\n| **App Geotag Summary** | Photo/video geotags with timestamps. |\n| **Integrity Log** | All hash values, acquisition timestamps. |\n\n---\n\n## 4.  Phase 3 \u2013 Analysis\n\n### 4.1. Build a Master Timeline\n\n| Activity | Tool | Why |\n|----------|------|-----|\n| Combine all extracted data into a *single chronological table* (GPS, Wi\u2011Fi, cell, app, system) | **Microsoft Excel**, **Google Sheets**, or **Auto\u2011Timeline** plugin in **FTK** | Provides a *holistic view* of device activity. |\n| Sort by timestamp, adjust for **time zone** and **clock drift** | **Chrono** script | Synchronizes logs from different sources. |\n\n### 4.2. Geo\u2011Reference All Points\n\n| Source | Method | Tool |\n|--------|---------|------|\n| **GPS coordinates** | Direct mapping to latitude/longitude. | **QGIS** (open\u2011source), **ArcGIS Online**, or **Google Earth**. |\n| **Wi\u2011Fi BSSID** | Query **Wi\u2011Fi Fingerprint** databases (Wi\u2011Fi\u2011DB, OpenCellID). | **WiFi\u2011DB API**, **OpenCellID**. |\n| **Cell Tower ID** | Look up **MCC/MNC/LAC/CID** in **OpenCellID**, **Mozilla Location Service**. | **CellMapper** API. |\n| **Knox logs** | Cross\u2011reference with GPS if available. | Same as GPS. |\n| **App geotags** | Use EXIF GPS tags. | **ExifTool**. |\n\n### 4.3. Correlate with the *Murder Scene*\n\n| Step | Tool | Justification |\n|------|------|---------------|\n| 1. Import the *crime scene address* (or coordinates) into GIS. | **QGIS** | Provides a *spatial overlay* of device locations. |\n| 2. Create a *buffer zone* (e.g., 50\u202fm, 100\u202fm) around the scene. | **QGIS** | Defines a *reasonable proximity* considering GPS accuracy. |\n| 3. Identify all location points falling within the buffer on **15\u202fJan\u202f2024**. | **QGIS** | Visual evidence of presence. |\n| 4. Map *time stamps* to the *timeline* of the murder (e.g., 20:00\u201321:00). | **Excel** | Shows whether the device was *inside* the buffer during the key window. |\n| 5. Cross\u2011check *Wi\u2011Fi/BSSID* data to ensure the device was *connected* to a known access point at the crime scene. | **Wi\u2011Fi\u2011DB** | Adds confidence. |\n| 6. Cross\u2011check *cell tower* logs for the same period. | **CellMapper** | Provides additional confirmation. |\n\n### 4.4. Evaluate Credibility of the Data\n\n| Criterion | How to Verify | Notes |\n|------------|---------------|-------|\n| **Timestamp accuracy** | Compare against *system clock* (device's `Settings \u2192 About phone \u2192 System time`). | If the clock was manipulated, adjust. |\n| **Accuracy values** | GPS `accuracy` field (meters). | Disregard points with accuracy > 200\u202fm. |\n| **Device usage pattern** | Correlate with *app usage* (e.g., navigation app). | If a user was actively navigating, location updates are more reliable. |\n| **Consistency** | Cross\u2011check GPS vs Wi\u2011Fi vs cell. | If all three point to the same location, confidence increases. |\n| **Physical evidence** | Compare with *other evidence* (e.g., CCTV, witness statements). | Helps corroborate the digital findings. |\n\n### 4.5. Summary of Findings\n\nCreate a **conclusion** that directly answers the investigative question:\n\n> *\u201cBased on the GPS coordinates, Wi\u2011Fi/BSSID, and cell tower data extracted from the Samsung\u202fS23, the suspect\u2019s device was located at **[Exact Address]** between **[Start]** and **[End]** on 15\u202fJan\u202f2024, which overlaps with the timeline of the murder.\u201d*\n\nInclude clear *confidence levels* (high, medium, low) and explain any *limitations* (e.g., gaps in data, possible spoofing).\n\n---\n\n## 5. Verification** | List of hash values, verification logs. | Shows *data integrity*. |\n| **Evidence Inventory** | Table of partitions, files, sizes, extraction dates. | Transparent *data provenance*. |\n| **Location Data Tables** | CSV/Excel tables with timestamps, lat/lon, accuracy, provider. | Core evidence. |\n| **Geospatial Maps** | GIS screenshots of device locations overlaid on crime scene. Discuss missing data, potential spoofing, GPS errors. | Provides *full disclosure*. |\n| **Conclusion** | Direct answer to the investigative question, with confidence level. | Final verdict. |\n| **Appendices** | Tool logs, raw data excerpts, code snippets, reference material. | Allows *peer review* and *re\u2011analysis*. |\n| **Signature & Certification** | Forensic examiner\u2019s signature, date, and certification. | Legal requirement. |\n\n### Tips for a Defensible Report\n\n1. **Use Forensic\u2011Ready Formats** \u2013 Export tables in *CSV* (human readable) and *PDF* Introduction & Legal Context  \n\n| Item | Detail |\n|------|--------|\n| **Case objective** | Establish the *geographical position* of the suspect on **15\u202fJan\u202f2024** (the day of the homicide). |\n| **Device under scrutiny** | Samsung Galaxy\u202fS23 (Android\u00a014, 256\u202fGB, fully encrypted, Samsung\u202fKnox\u202fenabled). |\n| **Legal basis** | Forensic acquisition and examination performed under a valid search warrant / subpoena. All actions must respect the **U.S. Federal Rules of Evidence** (Rule\u00a0901), **NIST\u202f800\u201186** guidelines and the **APIS** (Acquisition, Processing, Analysis, and Reporting Standards). |\n| **NIST 4\u2011Phase Model** | 1) **Collection** \u2013 secure, seize, image. <br>2) **Examination** \u2013 verify integrity, inventory, file system mapping. <br>3) **Analysis** \u2013 data\u2011parsing, timeline construction, geolocation mapping. <br>4) **Reporting** \u2013 chain of custody, methodology, findings, conclusions. |\n\n> **Why NIST?**  \n> The four\u2011phase framework enforces a **structured, repeatable, defensible** process that allows the court to evaluate the validity of the evidence. Each step has built\u2011in auditability (hashes, logs, chain of custody) and aligns with the **Digital Evidence and Forensics (DEF) Toolkit** used by most U.S. agencies.\n\n---\n\n## 2.  Phase 1 \u2013 Collection\n\n| Step | What to Do | Why It Matters | Suggested Tools |\n|------|-------------|----------------|-----------------|\n| **2.1. Evidence Preparation** | \u2022 Document *device* (IMEI, serial, model). <br>\u2022 Photograph the device in situ (front, side, power button). <br>\u2022 Record *witness statements* (if any). | Establishes **context** and a baseline for later comparison. | Smartphone camera, field logbook, chain\u2011of\u2011custody sheet. |\n| **2.2. Physical Acquisition (Full Digital Image)** | \u2022 Power\u2011off the phone (if possible). <br>\u2022 Remove the **SD\u2011card** (if present). <br>\u2022 Connect to a **JTAG/EDL** adapter (Samsung\u00a0S23 uses *Fastboot* or *EDL*). <br>\u2022 Extract the **bootloader, system, userdata, cache** partitions. | Captures *all* data, including deleted files, hidden partitions, and protected storage (Knox, EFS). | \u2022 **Cellebrite Physical Analyzer** (supports Samsung\u00a0S23 / Knox). <br>\u2022 **Oxygen Forensics Physical Analyzer** (supports full\u2011partition image). <br>\u2022 **Magnet AXIOM** (EDL/FASTBOOT support). |\n| **2.3. Logical Acquisition (If Device Is Unlocked)** | \u2022 Enable **USB debugging**. <br>\u2022 Pull the *data* partition via **ADB** (`adb pull`). <br>\u2022 Pull *Google Play Services* databases, *Location Services* caches, *app data* (WhatsApp, Instagram, Telegram). | Provides a *quick* snapshot with minimal wear on the device. | **ADB**, **Cellebrite UFED** (logical mode), **Oxygen** (logical mode). |\n| **2.4. Cloud & Account\u2011Based Data** | \u2022 Request *Google Account* \u201cLocation History\u201d via **Google Takeout**. <br>\u2022 Request *Samsung Cloud* backups (via Samsung\u2019s \u201cFind My Mobile\u201d). | Some location data is stored on the cloud and may survive a factory reset or encryption of the local storage. | **Google Takeout**, **Samsung Cloud** interface. |\n| **2.5. Integrity Verification** | \u2022 Compute **SHA\u2011256** (and MD5) for every image / file created. <br>\u2022 Store hash values in a *tamper\u2011proof* log (e.g., immutable ledger, write\u2011once\u2011read\u2011many disk). | Ensures that the evidence has not been altered between acquisition and analysis. | **Hashdeep**, **FTK Imager**, **Aegis** (chain\u2011of\u2011custody). |\n| **2.6. Chain of Custody Documentation** | \u2022 Record *person* acquiring, *time*, *location*, *method*, *storage* conditions. <br>\u2022 Sign and store the chain\u2011of\u2011custody sheet in a *tamper\u2011evident* envelope. | Required by law to prove admissibility. | Chain\u2011of\u2011custody template, digital signature. |\n\n### Key Considerations for the S23\n\n| Issue | Mitigation |\n|-------|------------|\n| **Device encryption** (Android Keystore + Knox) | Use *Knox\u2011enabled* forensic tools that can read the **Knox EFS** and **Secure Boot** partitions. |\n| **Secure Boot & Verified Boot** | Verify that the bootloader signatures match Samsung\u2019s official keys; any mismatch indicates tampering. |\n| **Remote wipe** | Verify that the device was not remotely wiped (e.g., \u201cFind My Mobile\u201d \u2192 \u201cErase\u201d). |\n| **Battery state** | Record battery level; low battery may affect logging. |\n\n---\n\n## 3.  Phase 2 \u2013 Examination\n\nThe goal of Examination is to **inventory** the acquired data and locate *all sources* that can provide location information.\n\n| Step | Activity | Justification | Tools |\n|------|----------|---------------|-------|\n| **3.1. Verify Acquisition Integrity** | \u2022 Re\u2011hash each image/file. <br>\u2022 Compare with stored hashes. | Confirms that the acquisition was *intact* before any processing. | **Hashdeep**, **FTK Imager**. |\n| **3.2. File System Mapping** | \u2022 Mount the *userdata* ext4 image. <br>\u2022 Use *file system forensics* to list directories, timestamps. | Identifies where Android stores *location logs* and *app data*. | **Autopsy**, **FTK**, **Mount\u2011Windows / ext4**. |\n| **3.3. Identify Location\u2011Related Databases** | \u2022 Search for: `fused_location_provider`, `LocationManager`, `GooglePlayServices`, `com.google.android.gms.location`. <br>\u2022 Search for *SQLite* databases with location tables (`locations`, `history`). | The core of Android\u2019s location service is stored here. | **SQLite3**, **Autopsy SQLite plugin**, **Magnet AXIOM**. |\n| **3.4. Extract GPS Coordinates** | \u2022 Parse the `fused_location_provider` DB \u2192 `location` table (lat, lon, accuracy, provider, timestamp). <br>\u2022 Parse `Google Maps` cache (e.g., `maps.db`, `timeline.db`). | Provides *raw* latitude/longitude with timestamps. | **Custom Python/SQLite scripts** (pandas), **Oxygen**. |\n| **3.5. Extract Wi\u2011Fi & Cell Tower Records** | \u2022 Parse `/data/misc/wifi/wpa_supplicant.conf` and `/data/misc/wifi/wifi.log`. <br>\u2022 Extract BSSID/SSID, signal strength, timestamp. <br>\u2022 Parse `telephony` logs for `CellTower` IDs, LAC, CID, PSC. | Wi\u2011Fi BSSID and cell IDs can be *geo\u2011referenced* using public databases. | **Wireshark** (for log parsing), **OpenCellID** API, **Mozilla Location Service**. |\n| **3.6. Extract Samsung Knox logs** | \u2022 Pull `knox_efs` and `knox_log` directories. <br>\u2022 Look for `device_location` tables. | Knox may store *additional* location data in a protected partition. | **Knox SDK** (for forensic extraction), **Cellebrite**. |\n| **3.7. Extract Third\u2011Party App Geotags** | \u2022 Parse `WhatsApp/Media/WhatsApp\u00a0Images` for EXIF GPS. <br>\u2022 Parse `Telegram` media metadata. <br>\u2022 Parse `Instagram` caches for media geotags. | App data may contain *user\u2011generated* location evidence (e.g., photos, messages). | **ExifTool**, **Oxygen**, **FTK**. |\n| **3.8. Extract Logcat & System Logs** | \u2022 Pull `/data/misc/logcat/` and `logcat.log`. <br>\u2022 Search for `LocationManager`, `FusedLocationProvider`. | Logs often contain *timestamped* location updates even if the DB is deleted. | **Logcat Viewer**, **Autopsy**. |\n| **3.9. Extract Battery & Sensor Data** | \u2022 Pull `/data/system/batterystats.xml`. <br>\u2022 Look for *battery discharges* that coincide with location updates. | Helps confirm device activity at specific times. | **BatteryStats Analyzer**. |\n| **3.10. Cross\u2011Check Timestamps** | \u2022 Convert all timestamps to *UTC* and to the **local time zone** of the suspect (if known). | Avoids mis\u2011interpretation of location windows. | **Chrono**, **Python datetime**. |\n\n### Deliverables from Examination\n\n| Deliverable | Content |\n|--------------|---------|\n| **Device Inventory** | List of partitions, files, sizes, timestamps. |\n| **Extracted Location Tables** | CSV/Excel file with `datetime`, `lat`, `lon`, `accuracy`, `provider`. |\n| **Wi\u2011Fi & Cell Tower Logs** | BSSID/SSID, LAC/CID, timestamps. |\n| **Knox Log Summary** | Any location events. |\n| **App Geotag Summary** | Photo/video geotags with timestamps. |\n| **Integrity Log** | All hash values, acquisition timestamps. |\n\n---\n\n## 4.  Phase 3 \u2013 Analysis\n\n### 4.1. Build a Master Timeline\n\n| Activity | Tool | Why |\n|----------|------|-----|\n| Combine all extracted data into a *single chronological table* (GPS, Wi\u2011Fi, cell, app, system) | **Microsoft Excel**, **Google Sheets**, or **Auto\u2011Timeline** plugin in **FTK** | Provides a *holistic view* of device activity. |\n| Sort by timestamp, adjust for **time zone** and **clock drift** | **Chrono** script | Synchronizes logs from different sources. |\n\n### 4.2. Geo\u2011Reference All Points\n\n| Source | Method | Tool |\n|--------|---------|------|\n| **GPS coordinates** | Direct mapping to latitude/longitude. | **QGIS** (open\u2011source), **ArcGIS Online**, or **Google Earth**. |\n| **Wi\u2011Fi BSSID** | Query **Wi\u2011Fi Fingerprint** databases (Wi\u2011Fi\u2011DB, OpenCellID). | **WiFi\u2011DB API**, **OpenCellID**. |\n| **Cell Tower ID** | Look up **MCC/MNC/LAC/CID** in **OpenCellID**, **Mozilla Location Service**. | **CellMapper** API. |\n| **Knox logs** | Cross\u2011reference with GPS if available. | Same as GPS. |\n| **App geotags** | Use EXIF GPS tags. | **ExifTool**. |\n\n### 4.3. Correlate with the *Murder Scene*\n\n| Step | Tool | Justification |\n|------|------|---------------|\n| 1. Import the *crime scene address* (or coordinates) into GIS. | **QGIS** | Provides a *spatial overlay* of device locations. |\n| 2. Create a *buffer zone* (e.g., 50\u202fm, 100\u202fm) around the scene. | **QGIS** | Defines a *reasonable proximity* considering GPS accuracy. |\n| 3. Identify all location points falling within the buffer on **15\u202fJan\u202f2024**. | **QGIS** | Visual evidence of presence. |\n| 4. Map *time stamps* to the *timeline* of the murder (e.g., 20:00\u201321:00). | **Excel** | Shows whether the device was *inside* the buffer during the key window. |\n| 5. Cross\u2011check *Wi\u2011Fi/BSSID* data to ensure the device was *connected* to a known access point at the crime scene. | **Wi\u2011Fi\u2011DB** | Adds confidence. |\n| 6. Cross\u2011check *cell tower* logs for the same period. | **CellMapper** | Provides additional confirmation. |\n\n### 4.4. Evaluate Credibility of the Data\n\n| Criterion | How to Verify | Notes |\n|------------|---------------|-------|\n| **Timestamp accuracy** | Compare against *system clock* (device's `Settings \u2192 About phone \u2192 System time`). | If the clock was manipulated, adjust. |\n| **Accuracy values** | GPS `accuracy` field (meters). | Disregard points with accuracy > 200\u202fm. |\n| **Device usage pattern** | Correlate with *app usage* (e.g., navigation app). | If a user was actively navigating, location updates are more reliable. |\n| **Consistency** | Cross\u2011check GPS vs Wi\u2011Fi vs cell. | If all three point to the same location, confidence increases. |\n| **Physical evidence** | Compare with *other evidence* (e.g., CCTV, witness statements). | Helps corroborate the digital findings. |\n\n### 4.5. Summary of Findings\n\nCreate a **conclusion** that directly answers the investigative question:\n\n> *\u201cBased on the GPS coordinates, Wi\u2011Fi/BSSID, and cell tower data extracted from the Samsung\u202fS23, the suspect\u2019s device was located at **[Exact Address]** between **[Start]** and **[End]** on 15\u202fJan\u202f2024, which overlaps with the timeline of the murder.\u201d*\n\nInclude clear *confidence levels* (high, medium, low) and explain any *limitations* (e.g., gaps in data, possible spoofing).\n\n---\n\n## 5. reference. |\n| **Background & Scope** | Case number, objective, scope of device. | Sets context. |\n| **Methodology** | Detailed description of each phase, tools used, validation steps. | |\n| **Location Data Tables** | CSV/Excel tables with timestamps, lat/lon, accuracy, provider. | Core evidence. |\n| **Geospatial Maps** | GIS screenshots of device locations overlaid on crime scene. **Appendices** | Tool logs, raw data excerpts, code snippets, reference material. | Allows *peer review* and *re\u2011analysis*. |\n| **Signature & Certification** | Forensic examiner\u2019s signature, date, and certification. | Legal requirement. |\n\n### Tips for a Defensible Report\n\n1. **Use Forensic\u2011Ready Formats** \u2013 Export tables in *CSV* (human readable) and *PDF* (non\u2011editable).  \n2. **Include Digital Signatures** \u2013 Sign the PDF with a *Genuine Digital Signature* (GDS).  \n3. **Maintain a Detailed Audit Trail** \u2013 Each tool used must log its actions (e.g., Cellebrite\u2019s \u201cActivity Log\u201d).  \n4. **Preserve Original Evidence** \u2013 All images and logs must remain untouched; work on *forensic copies* only.  \n5. **Peer Review** \u2013 Have a second examiner verify the analysis.  \n\n---\n\n## 6. Potential Pitfalls & Mitigation\n\n| Pitfall | Mitigation |\n|---------|------------|\n| **Device was factory reset** | Use **Google Takeout** location history; look for *Android* `Google Play Services` cached logs. |\n| **Location services disabled** | Look for *last known location* in `fused_location_provider`. |\n| **GPS spoofing / VPN** | Correlate with *cell tower* and *Wi\u2011Fi* data; inconsistency suggests spoofing. |\n| **Clock manipulation** | Cross\u2011check with *system logs* and *external time sources* (e.g., Wi\u2011Fi BSSID timestamps). |\n| **Encrypted data** | Use *Knox* extraction; if inaccessible, document limitation. |\n| **Missing or incomplete logs** | Note gaps; consider *alternative evidence* (CCTV, witnesses). |\n| **Legal restrictions on cloud data** | Obtain proper *subpoena* before accessing Google/Samsung cloud accounts. |\n\n---\n\n## 8. NIST 4\u2011Phase Overview\n\n| Phase | Core Purpose | Key Deliverable |\n|-------|--------------|-----------------|\n| **Collection** | Securely acquire the device and all related evidence while preserving integrity. | Forensic image(s), chain of custody log, metadata. |\n| **Examination** | Identify, extract, and preserve relevant data (location, logs, apps, communications). | Raw data sets, extracted artifacts, hash values. |\n| **Analysis** | Interpret the extracted data, build a timeline, map geospatial points, and correlate with external sources. | Timeline, geospatial map, correlation matrix, hypothesis. |\n| **Reporting** | Compile findings into a clear, legally admissible report and prepare for court presentation. | Final report, expert testimony notes, evidence list. |\n\n---\n\n## 2. Phase 1 \u2013 Collection\n\n| Step | Action | Justification | Recommended Tool(s) |\n|------|--------|---------------|---------------------|\n| **2.1 Evidence Identification** | \u2022 Document device model, OS version, serial number, IMEI, battery level.<br>\u2022 Identify all removable media (SIM, micro\u2011SD, external storage). | Establishes baseline and ensures nothing is missed. | None (manual). |\n| **2.2 Chain of Custody** | \u2022 Create a signed chain of custody form (EID, date/time, handlers, conditions).<br>\u2022 Store evidence in tamper\u2011evident bags, label with unique ID. | Legal requirement; preserves admissibility. | Standard forensic evidence kit. |\n| **2.3 Physical Acquisition (if possible)** | \u2022 Use a write\u2011blocker compatible with Android (e.g., Cellebrite UFED Physical Analyzer, Oxygen Forensics Physical).<br>\u2022 Perform a bit\u2011by\u2011bit image of internal storage (eMMC).<br>\u2022 Verify integrity with SHA\u2011256. | Provides the most complete data set; preserves hidden/undeleted files. | **Cellebrite UFED Physical Analyzer** (supports Samsung S23), **Oxygen Forensics Detective** (physical mode). |\n| **2.4 Logical Acquisition** | \u2022 If the device is locked or physical acquisition is infeasible, use a logical extraction (USB\u2011debug mode, ADB, or forensic app).<br>\u2022 Capture: contacts, SMS, call logs, app data, Wi\u2011Fi SSIDs, Bluetooth, GPS logs, Google/ Samsung location history, system logs. | Logical extraction is less invasive and often the only viable option on a locked device. | **Cellebrite UFED Logical**, **Oxygen Forensics Detective**, **Magnet AXIOM**, **Elcomsoft Phone Viewer**. |\n| **2.5 SIM & Cloud Acquisition** | \u2022 Read SIM card with a forensic reader (e.g., Cellebrite Smart\u2011SIM).<br>\u2022 Request Google Takeout / Samsung Cloud backup (if available) via court order. | SIM contains call/SMS logs; cloud may hold location history and app data. | **Cellebrite Smart\u2011SIM**, **Google Takeout**, **Samsung Cloud**. |\n| **2.6 Documentation** | \u2022 Log all acquisition steps, tools, settings, timestamps.<br>\u2022 Capture photographs of the device, packaging, and environment. | Provides audit trail and supports later validation. | Standard forensic documentation. |\n\n**Notes on Encryption & Remote Wipe**\n\n- If the device is encrypted (default on S23), attempt to unlock using the passcode or pattern supplied by the suspect (if available).  \n- If the device was remotely wiped (Find My Mobile, Samsung Knox), capture the \u201cremote wipe\u201d log from `/data/system/` or from the cloud.  \n- If unlocking is impossible, use tools that can recover the encryption key from the device\u2019s hardware (e.g., **Elcomsoft Phone Breaker** for Android).\n\n---\n\n## 3. Phase 2 \u2013 Examination\n\n| Step | Action | Justification | Recommended Tool(s) |\n|------|--------|---------------|---------------------|\n| **3.1 Verify Image Integrity** | \u2022 Re\u2011hash the forensic image and compare to the original hash. | Confirms no tampering during acquisition. | **HashCalc**, **FTK Imager**. |\n| **3.2 File System Analysis** | \u2022 Mount the image (e.g., Autopsy, Sleuth Kit).<br>\u2022 Identify partitions: `/system`, `/data`, `/cache`, `/sdcard`. | Locates where location data and logs reside. | **Autopsy**, **The Sleuth Kit (TSK)**. |\n| **3.3 Location Data Extraction** | \u2022 **GPS logs**: `/data/system/location/` (e.g., `gps.log`, `location.log`).<br>\u2022 **Google Location History**: `com.google.android.gms` database (`LocationHistory.db`).<br>\u2022 **Samsung Location History**: `com.samsung.android.location` database (`LocationHistory.db`).<br>\u2022 **App\u2011specific logs**: Uber, Lyft, Waze, Google Maps Timeline, etc. | These files contain raw latitude/longitude with timestamps. | **Cellebrite UFED**, **Oxygen Forensics**, **Magnet AXIOM**, **Elcomsoft Phone Viewer** (supports SQLite). |\n| **3.4 System & Service Logs** | \u2022 `logcat` dumps (`/data/system/logcat/`).<br>\u2022 `dumpsys` outputs for `location`, `wifi`, `telephony`. | Provides context (e.g., Wi\u2011Fi association, cell tower changes). | **ADB** (if unlocked), **Cellebrite**, **Oxygen**. |\n| **3.5 Network & Connectivity Data** | \u2022 Wi\u2011Fi SSIDs, BSSIDs, signal strength, timestamps.<br>\u2022 Cell tower IDs (LAC, CID, PSC).<br>\u2022 Bluetooth device names/addresses. | Enables triangulation when GPS is unavailable. | **Cellebrite**, **Oxygen**, **Wireshark** (for captured packets). |\n| **3.6 App & Service Artifacts** | \u2022 Extract data from: Google Maps, Waze, Uber, Lyft, Samsung Health, Samsung SmartThings, Samsung Pay, Samsung Notes, Bixby, Knox, Secure Folder. | Some apps store their own location history or logs. | **Cellebrite**, **Oxygen**, **Magnet AXIOM**. |\n| **3.7 Metadata & Timestamps** | \u2022 File system timestamps (created, modified, accessed).<br>\u2022 Android `content://` URIs for location. | Helps verify authenticity and detect tampering. | **Autopsy**, **FTK**, **SQLite Browser**. |\n| **3.8 Data Preservation** | \u2022 Export all extracted artifacts to a separate, write\u2011protected repository.<br>\u2022 Store hash values for each file. | Prevents accidental alteration of evidence. | Standard forensic storage. |\n\n---\n\n## 4. Phase 3 \u2013 Analysis\n\n| Step | Action | Justification | Recommended Tool(s) |\n|------|--------|---------------|---------------------|\n| **4.1 Timeline Construction** | \u2022 Combine all timestamps (GPS, logs, app events, system logs).<br>\u2022 Use chronological ordering to identify movement patterns. | Establishes when and where the suspect was at specific times. | **Timeline Explorer** (part of **Cellebrite**), **Magnet AXIOM**, **FTK**, **Log2timeline**. |\n| **4.2 Geospatial Mapping** | \u2022 Import GPS coordinates into GIS software.<br>\u2022 Overlay with street maps, cell tower locations, Wi\u2011Fi hotspots. | Visualizes movement and potential routes. | **QGIS**, **ArcGIS**, **Google Earth Pro**. |\n| **4.3 Correlation with External Sources** | \u2022 Cross\u2011check device location with:<br>\u2003\u2013 Police GPS data (e.g., traffic cameras, CCTV geotags).<br>\u2003\u2013 Mobile network operator (MNO) records (CDR, BTS).<br>\u2003\u2013 Cloud backups (Google Maps Timeline, Samsung Cloud).<br>\u2003\u2013 Witness statements. | Strengthens evidence and rules out false positives. | **OpenCellID**, **CellMapper**, **Google Maps Timeline** (via Takeout), **MNO CDR extraction** (via court order). |\n| **4.4 Anomaly & Anti\u2011Forensics Detection** | \u2022 Look for signs of location spoofing (e.g., sudden jumps, inconsistent timestamps).<br>\u2022 Verify integrity of logs (hashes, file system metadata). | Ensures conclusions are based on authentic data. | **Cellebrite**, **Oxygen**, **Autopsy** (for file integrity). |\n| **4.5 Hypothesis Generation & Testing** | \u2022 Formulate hypotheses (e.g., suspect was at Scene A from 10:00\u201310:15).<br>\u2022 Test against all data sources. | Provides a structured narrative for the report. | None (analytical). |\n| **4.6 Documentation of Findings** | \u2022 Record all steps, tools, settings, and results.<br>\u2022 Capture screenshots, export tables. | Required for reproducibility and court admissibility. | **Microsoft Word**, **Adobe PDF**, **Excel**. |\n\n---\n\n## 5. Phase 4 \u2013 Reporting\n\n| Step | Action | Justification | Recommended Tool(s) |\n|------|--------|---------------|---------------------|\n| **5.1 Report Structure** | \u2022 Executive summary.<br>\u2022 Methodology (NIST phases, tools, chain of custody).<br>\u2022 Findings (timeline, maps, artifacts).<br>\u2022 Conclusions (location on 15\u202fJan\u202f2024).<br>\u2022 Appendices (tool logs, hash lists, raw data excerpts). | Provides a clear, legally defensible narrative. | **Microsoft Word**, **Adobe Acrobat**. |\n| **5.2 Expert Testimony Preparation** | \u2022 Prepare slides, visual aids (maps, timelines).<br>\u2022 Rehearse explanation of tools and processes. | Ensures effective courtroom presentation. | **PowerPoint**, **QGIS** export, **Cellebrite** report export. |\n| **5.3 Evidence Management** | \u2022 Label all evidence files with unique IDs.<br>\u2022 Store copies in secure, access\u2011controlled environment. | Maintains integrity for future appeals. | Standard evidence storage. |\n| **5.4 Review & Quality Assurance** | \u2022 Peer review of report and findings.<br>\u2022 Verify all calculations and map coordinates. | Reduces risk of errors that could be challenged. | Internal QA checklist. |\n\n---\n\n## 6. Legal & Ethical Considerations\n\n| Issue | Mitigation |\n|-------|------------|\n| **Privacy** | Only collect data directly relevant to the investigation. Obtain court orders for cloud data. |\n| **Admissibility** | Follow chain of custody, use validated tools, document all steps, preserve original evidence. |\n| **Data Protection** | Store all personal data in encrypted, access\u2011controlled storage. |\n| **Cross\u2011Border Data** | If cloud data is stored abroad, ensure compliance with GDPR/CCPA and obtain necessary warrants. |\n| **Anti\u2011Forensics** | Verify integrity of logs, check for tampering, use hash verification. |\n\n---\n\n## 7. Potential Challenges & Mitigation Strategies\n\n| Challenge | Likely Impact | Mitigation |\n|-----------|---------------|------------|\n| **Device Encryption** | Prevents logical extraction. | Use **Elcomsoft Phone Breakory** or **Cellebrite**\u2019s \u201cAndroid Encryption Bypass\u201d if passcode is known; otherwise, rely on cloud backups. |\n| **Remote Wipe** | Deletes local data. | Capture remote\u2011wipe logs, request MNO for CDRs, use cloud backups. |\n| **Location Spoofing** | Falsifies GPS coordinates. | Cross\u2011check with Wi\u2011Fi/BTS data, verify timestamp consistency, look for anomalies in log files. |\n| **App Data Encryption** | Some apps encrypt their own databases. | Use **Cellebrite** or **Oxygen**\u2019s app\u2011specific modules; if impossible, rely on system logs or cloud sync. |\n| **Data Volume** | Large amount of irrelevant data. | Use filtering (date range, app names) early in extraction; focus on 15\u202fJan\u202f2024. |\n| **Legal Restrictions** | Limited access to certain data (e.g., SIM, cloud). | Obtain proper warrants, use subpoenas, coordinate with telecom providers. |\n\n---\n\n## 8.         "text_final": "<|start|>assistant<|channel|>final<|message|>## Digital Forensics Methodology for the Samsung\u202fS23  \n### Objective  \nDetermine the suspect's physical location on **15\u202fJanuary\u202f2024** (the day of the murder) using the seized Samsung\u202fS23, following the NIST 4\u2011Phase Model (Collection \u2192 Examination \u2192 Analysis \u2192 Reporting).\n\n---\n\n### 1. NIST 4\u2011Phase Overview\n\n| Phase | Core Purpose | Key Deliverable |\n|-------|--------------|-----------------|\n| **Collection** | Securely acquire the device and all related evidence while preserving integrity. | Forensic image(s), chain of custody log, metadata. |\n| **Examination** | Identify, extract, and preserve relevant data (location, logs, apps, communications). | Raw data sets, extracted artifacts, hash values. |\n| **Analysis** | Interpret the extracted data, build a timeline, map geospatial points, and correlate with external sources. | Timeline, geospatial map, correlation matrix, hypothesis. |\n| **Reporting** | Compile findings into a clear, legally admissible report and prepare for court presentation. | Final report, expert testimony notes, evidence list. |\n\n---\n\n## 2. Phase 1 \u2013 Collection\n\n| Step | Action | Justification | Recommended Tool(s) |\n|------|--------|---------------|---------------------|\n| **2.1 Evidence Identification** | \u2022 Document device model, OS version, serial number, IMEI, battery level.<br>\u2022 Identify all removable media (SIM, micro\u2011SD, external storage). | Establishes baseline and ensures nothing is missed. | None (manual). |\n| **2.2 Chain of Custody** | \u2022 Create a signed chain of custody form (EID, date/time, handlers, conditions).<br>\u2022 Store evidence in tamper\u2011evident bags, label with unique ID. | Legal requirement; preserves admissibility. | Standard forensic evidence kit. |\n| **2.3 Physical Acquisition (if possible)** | \u2022 Use a write\u2011blocker compatible with Android (e.g., Cellebrite UFED Physical Analyzer, Oxygen Forensics Physical).<br>\u2022 Perform a bit\u2011by\u2011bit image of internal storage (eMMC).<br>\u2022 Verify integrity with SHA\u2011256. | Provides the most complete data set; preserves hidden/undeleted files. | **Cellebrite UFED Physical Analyzer** (supports Samsung S23), **Oxygen Forensics Detective** (physical mode). |\n| **2.4 Logical Acquisition** | \u2022 If the device is locked or physical acquisition is infeasible, use a logical extraction (USB\u2011debug mode, ADB, or forensic app).<br>\u2022 Capture: contacts, SMS, call logs, app data, Wi\u2011Fi SSIDs, Bluetooth, GPS logs, Google/ Samsung location history, system logs. | Logical extraction is less invasive and often the only viable option on a locked device. | **Cellebrite UFED Logical**, **Oxygen Forensics Detective**, **Magnet AXIOM**, **Elcomsoft Phone Viewer**. |\n| **2.5 SIM & Cloud Acquisition** | \u2022 Read SIM card with a forensic reader (e.g., Cellebrite Smart\u2011SIM).<br>\u2022 Request Google Takeout / Samsung Cloud backup (if available) via court order. | SIM contains call/SMS logs; cloud may hold location history and app data. | **Cellebrite Smart\u2011SIM**, **Google Takeout**, **Samsung Cloud**. |\n| **2.6 Documentation** | \u2022 Log all acquisition steps, tools, settings, timestamps.<br>\u2022 Capture photographs of the device, packaging, and environment. | Provides audit trail and supports later validation. | Standard forensic documentation. |\n\n**Notes on Encryption & Remote Wipe**\n\n- If the device is encrypted (default on S23), attempt to unlock using the passcode or pattern supplied by the suspect (if available).  \n- If the device was remotely wiped (Find My Mobile, Samsung Knox), capture the \u201cremote wipe\u201d log from `/data/system/` or from the cloud.  \n- If unlocking is impossible, use tools that can recover the encryption key from the device\u2019s hardware (e.g., **Elcomsoft Phone Breaker** for Android).\n\n---\n\n## 3. Phase 2 \u2013 Examination\n\n| Step | Action | Justification | Recommended Tool(s) |\n|------|--------|---------------|---------------------|\n| **3.1 Verify Image Integrity** | \u2022 Re\u2011hash suspect's physical location on **15\u202fJanuary\u202f2024** (the day of the murder) using the seized Samsung\u202fS23, following the NIST 4\u2011Phase Model (Collection \u2192 Examination \u2192 Analysis \u2192 Reporting).\n\n---\n\n### 1. NIST 4\u2011Phase Overview\n\n| Phase | Core Purpose | Key Deliverable |\n|-------|--------------|-----------------|\n| **Collection** | Securely acquire the device and all related evidence while preserving integrity. | Forensic image(s), chain of custody log, metadata. |\n| **Examination** | Identify, extract, and preserve relevant data (location, logs, apps, communications). | Raw data sets, extracted artifacts, hash values. |\n| **Analysis** | Interpret the extracted data, build a timeline, map geospatial points, and correlate with external sources. | Timeline, geospatial map, correlation matrix, hypothesis. |\n| **Reporting** | Compile findings into a clear, legally admissible report and prepare for court presentation. | Final report, expert testimony notes, evidence list. |\n\n---\n\n## 2. Phase 1 \u2013 Collection\n\n| Step | Action | Justification | Recommended Tool(s) |\n|------|--------|---------------|---------------------|\n| **2.1 Evidence Identification** | \u2022 Document device model, OS version, serial number, IMEI, battery level.<br>\u2022 Identify all removable media (SIM, micro\u2011SD, external storage). | Establishes baseline and ensures nothing is missed. | None (manual). |\n| **2.2 Chain of Custody** | \u2022 Create a signed chain of custody form (EID, date/time, handlers, conditions).<br>\u2022 Store evidence in tamper\u2011evident bags, label with unique ID. | Legal requirement; preserves admissibility. | Standard forensic evidence kit. |\n| **2.3 Physical Acquisition (if possible)** | \u2022 Use a write\u2011blocker compatible with Android (e.g., Cellebrite UFED Physical Analyzer, Oxygen Forensics Physical).<br>\u2022 Perform a bit\u2011by\u2011bit image of internal storage (eMMC).<br>\u2022 Verify integrity with SHA\u2011256. | Provides the most complete data set; preserves hidden/undeleted files. | **Cellebrite UFED Physical Analyzer** (supports Samsung S23), **Oxygen Forensics Detective** (physical mode). |\n| **2.4 Logical Acquisition** | \u2022 If the device is locked or physical acquisition is infeasible, use a logical extraction (USB\u2011debug mode, ADB, or forensic app).<br>\u2022 Capture: contacts, SMS, call logs, app data, Wi\u2011Fi SSIDs, Bluetooth, GPS logs, Google/ Samsung location history, system logs. | Logical extraction is less invasive and often the only viable option on a locked device. | **Cellebrite UFED Logical**, **Oxygen Forensics Detective**, **Magnet AXIOM**, **Elcomsoft Phone Viewer**. |\n| **2.5 SIM & Cloud Acquisition** | \u2022 Read SIM card with a forensic reader (e.g., Cellebrite Smart\u2011SIM).<br>\u2022 Request Google Takeout / Samsung Cloud backup (if available) via court order. | SIM contains call/SMS logs; cloud may hold location history and app data. | **Cellebrite Smart\u2011SIM**, **Google Takeout**, **Samsung Cloud**. |\n| **2.6 Documentation** | \u2022 Log all acquisition steps, tools, settings, timestamps.<br>\u2022 Capture photographs of the device, packaging, and environment. | Provides audit trail and supports later validation. | Standard forensic documentation. |\n\n**Notes on Encryption & Remote Wipe**\n\n- If the device is encrypted (default on S23), attempt to unlock using the passcode or pattern supplied by the suspect (if available).  \n- If the device was remotely wiped (Find My Mobile, Samsung Knox), capture the \u201cremote wipe\u201d log from `/data/system/` or from the cloud.  \n- If unlocking is impossible, use tools that can recover the encryption key from the device\u2019s hardware (e.g., **Elcomsoft Phone Breaker** for Android).\n\n---\n\n## 3. Phase 2 \u2013 Examination\n\n| Step | Action | Justification | Recommended Tool(s) |\n|------|--------|---------------|---------------------|\n| **3.1 Verify Image Integrity** | \u2022 Re\u2011hash the forensic image and compare to the original hash. | Confirms no tampering during acquisition. | **HashCalc**, **FTK Imager**. |\n| **3.2 File System Analysis** | \u2022 Mount the image (e.g., Autopsy, Sleuth Kit).<br>\u2022 Identify partitions: `/system`, `/data`, `/cache`, `/sdcard`. | Locates where location data and logs reside. | **Autopsy**, **The Sleuth Kit (TSK)**. |\n| **3.3 Location Data Extraction** | \u2022 **GPS logs**: `/data/system/location/` (e.g., `gps.log`, `location.log`).<br>\u2022 **Google Location History**: `com.google.android.gms` database (`LocationHistory.db`).<br>\u2022 **Samsung Location History**: `com.samsung.android.location` database (`LocationHistory.db`).<br>\u2022 **App\u2011specific logs**: Uber, Lyft, Waze, Google Maps Timeline, etc. | These files contain raw latitude/longitude with timestamps. | **Cellebrite UFED**, **Oxygen Forensics**, **Magnet AXIOM**, **Elcomsoft Phone Viewer** (supports SQLite). |\n| **3.4 System & Service Logs** | \u2022 `logcat` dumps (`/data/system/logcat/`).<br>\u2022 `dumpsys` outputs for `location`, `wifi`, `telephony`. | Provides context (e.g., Wi\u2011Fi association, cell tower changes). | **ADB** (if unlocked), **Cellebrite**, **Oxygen**. |\n| **3.5 Network & Connectivity Data** | \u2022 Wi\u2011Fi SSIDs, BSSIDs, signal strength, timestamps.<br>\u2022 Cell tower IDs (LAC, CID, PSC).<br>\u2022 Bluetooth device names/addresses. | Enables triangulation when GPS is unavailable. | **Cellebrite**, **Oxygen**, **Wireshark** (for captured packets). |\n| **3.6 App & Service Artifacts** | \u2022 Extract data from: Google Maps, Waze, Uber, Lyft, Samsung Health, Samsung SmartThings, Samsung Pay, Samsung Notes, Bixby, Knox, Secure Folder. | Some apps store their own location history or logs. | **Cellebrite**, **Oxygen**, **Magnet AXIOM**. |\n| **3.7 Metadata & Timestamps** | \u2022 File system timestamps (created, modified, accessed).<br>\u2022 Android `content://` URIs for location. | Helps verify authenticity and detect tampering. | **Autopsy**, **FTK**, **SQLite Browser**. |\n| **3.8 Data Preservation** | \u2022 Export all extracted artifacts to a separate,         "text_final": "<|start|>assistant<|channel|>final<|message|>## Digital Forensics Methodology for the Samsung\u202fS23  \n### Objective  \nDetermine the suspect's physical location on **15\u202fJanuary\u202f2024** (the day of the murder) using the seized Samsung\u202fS23, following the NIST 4\u2011Phase Model (Collection \u2192 Examination \u2192 Analysis \u2192 Reporting).\n\n---\n\n### 1. NIST 4\u2011Phase Overview\n\n| Phase | Core Purpose | Key Deliverable |\n|-------|--------------|-----------------|\n| **Collection** | Securely acquire the device and all related evidence while preserving integrity. | Forensic image(s), chain of custody log, metadata. |\n| **Examination** | Identify, extract, and preserve relevant data (location, logs, apps, communications). | Raw data sets, extracted artifacts, hash values. |\n| **Analysis** | Interpret the extracted data, build a timeline, map geospatial points, and correlate with external sources. | Timeline, geospatial map, correlation matrix, hypothesis. |\n| **Reporting** | Compile findings into a clear, legally admissible report and prepare for court presentation. | Final report, expert testimony notes, evidence list. |\n\n---\n\n## 2. Phase 1 \u2013 Collection\n\n| Step | Action | Justification | Recommended Tool(s) |\n|------|--------|---------------|---------------------|\n| **2.1 Evidence Identification** | \u2022 Document device model, OS version, serial number, IMEI, battery level.<br>\u2022 Identify all removable media (SIM, micro\u2011SD, external storage). | Establishes baseline and ensures nothing is missed. | None (manual). |\n| **2.2 Chain of Custody** | \u2022 Create a signed chain of custody form (EID, date/time, handlers, conditions).<br>\u2022 Store evidence in tamper\u2011evident bags, label with unique ID. | Legal requirement; preserves admissibility. | Standard forensic evidence kit. |\n| **2.3 Physical Acquisition (if possible)** | \u2022 Use a write\u2011blocker compatible with Android (e.g., Cellebrite UFED Physical Analyzer, Oxygen Forensics Physical).<br>\u2022 Perform a bit\u2011by\u2011bit image of internal storage (eMMC).<br>\u2022 Verify integrity with SHA\u2011256. | Provides the most complete data set; preserves hidden/undeleted files. | **Cellebrite UFED Physical Analyzer** (supports Samsung S23), **Oxygen Forensics Detective** (physical mode). |\n| **2.4 Logical Acquisition** | \u2022 If the device is locked or physical acquisition is infeasible, use a logical extraction (USB\u2011debug mode, ADB, or forensic app).<br>\u2022 Capture: contacts, SMS, call logs, app data, Wi\u2011Fi SSIDs, Bluetooth, GPS logs, Google/ Samsung location history, system logs. | Logical extraction is less invasive and often the only viable option on a locked device. | **Cellebrite UFED Logical**, **Oxygen Forensics Detective**, **Magnet AXIOM**, **Elcomsoft Phone Viewer**. |\n| **2.5 SIM & Cloud Acquisition** | \u2022 Read SIM card with a forensic reader (e.g., Cellebrite Smart\u2011SIM).<br>\u2022 Request Google Takeout / Samsung Cloud backup (if available) via court order. | SIM contains call/SMS logs; cloud may hold location history and app data. | **Cellebrite Smart\u2011SIM**, **Google Takeout**, **Samsung Cloud**. |\n| **2.6 Documentation** | \u2022 Log all acquisition steps, tools, settings, timestamps.<br>\u2022 Capture photographs of the device, packaging, and environment. | Provides audit trail and supports later validation. | Standard forensic documentation. |\n\n**Notes on Encryption & Remote Wipe**\n\n- If the device is encrypted (default on S23), attempt to unlock using the passcode or pattern supplied by the suspect (if available).  \n- If the device was remotely wiped (Find My Mobile, Samsung Knox), capture the \u201cremote wipe\u201d log from `/data/system/` or from the cloud.  \n- If unlocking is impossible, use tools that can recover the encryption key from the device\u2019s hardware (e.g., **Elcomsoft Phone Breaker** for Android).\n\n---\n\n## 3. Phase 2 \u2013 Examination\n\n| Step | Action | Justification | Recommended Tool(s) |\n|------|--------|---------------|---------------------|\n| **3.1 Verify Image Integrity** | \u2022 Re\u2011hash the forensic image and compare to the original hash. | Confirms no tampering during acquisition. | **HashCalc**, **FTK Imager**. |\n| **3.2 File System Analysis** | \u2022 Mount the image (e.g., Autopsy, Sleuth Kit).<br>\u2022 Identify partitions: `/system`, `/data`, `/cache`, `/sdcard`. | Locates where location data and logs reside. | **Autopsy**, **The Sleuth Kit (TSK)**. |\n| **3.3 Location Data Extraction** | \u2022 **GPS logs**: `/data/system/location/` (e.g., `gps.log`, `location.log`).<br>\u2022 **Google Location History**: `com.google.android.gms` database (`LocationHistory.db`).<br>\u2022 **Samsung Location History**: `com.samsung.android.location` database (`LocationHistory.db`).<br>\u2022 **App\u2011specific logs**: Uber, Lyft, Waze, Google Maps Timeline, etc. | These files contain raw latitude/longitude with timestamps. | **Cellebrite UFED**, **Oxygen Forensics**, **Magnet AXIOM**, **Elcomsoft Phone Viewer** (supports SQLite). |\n| **3.4 System & Service Logs** | \u2022 `logcat` dumps (`/data/system/logcat/`).<br>\u2022 `dumpsys` outputs for `location`, `wifi`, `telephony`. | Provides context (e.g., Wi\u2011Fi association, cell tower changes). | **ADB** (if unlocked), **Cellebrite**, **Oxygen**. |\n| **3.5 Network & Connectivity Data** | \u2022 Wi\u2011Fi SSIDs, BSSIDs, signal strength, timestamps.<br>\u2022 Cell tower IDs (LAC, CID, PSC).<br>\u2022 Bluetooth device names/addresses. | Enables triangulation when GPS is unavailable. | **Cellebrite**, **Oxygen**, **Wireshark** (for captured packets). |\n| **3.6 App & Service Artifacts** | \u2022 Extract data from: Google Maps, Waze, Uber, Lyft, Samsung Health, Samsung SmartThings, Samsung Pay, Samsung Notes, Bixby, Knox, Secure Folder. | Some apps store their own location history or logs. | **Cellebrite**, **Oxygen**, **Magnet AXIOM**. |\n| **3.7 Metadata & Timestamps** | \u2022 File system timestamps (created, modified, accessed).<br>\u2022 Android `content://` URIs for location. | Helps verify authenticity and detect tampering. | **Autopsy**, **FTK**, **SQLite Browser**. |\n| **3.8 Data Preservation** | \u2022 Export all extracted artifacts to a separate, write\u2011protected repository.<br>\u2022 Store hash values for each file. | Prevents accidental alteration of evidence. | Standard forensic storage. |\n\n---\n\n## 4. Phase 3 \u2013 Analysis\n\n| Step | Action | Justification | Recommended Tool(s) |\n|------|--------|---------------|---------------------|\n| **4.1 Timeline Construction** | \u2022 Combine all timestamps (GPS, logs, app events, system logs).<br>\u2022 Use chronological ordering to identify movement patterns. | Establishes when and where the suspect was at specific times. | **Timeline Explorer** (part of **Cellebrite**), **Magnet AXIOM**, **FTK**, **Log2timeline**. |\n| **4.2 Geospatial Mapping** | \u2022 Import GPS coordinates into GIS software.<br>\u2022 Overlay with street maps, cell tower locations, Wi\u2011Fi hotspots. | Visualizes movement and potential routes. | **QGIS**, **ArcGIS**, **Google Earth Pro**. |\n| **4.3 Correlation with External Sources** | \u2022 Cross\u2011check device location with:<br>\u2003\u2013 Police GPS data (e.g., traffic cameras, CCTV geotags).<br>\u2003\u2013 Mobile network operator (MNO) records (CDR, BTS).<br>\u2003\u2013 Cloud backups (Google Maps Timeline, Samsung Cloud).<br>\u2003\u2013 Witness statements. | Strengthens evidence and rules out false positives. | **OpenCellID**, **CellMapper**, **Google Maps Timeline** (via Takeout), **MNO CDR extraction** (via court order). |\n| **4.4 Anomaly & Anti\u2011Forensics Detection** | \u2022 Look for signs of location spoofing (e.g., sudden jumps, inconsistent timestamps).<br>\u2022 Verify integrity of logs (hashes, file system metadata). | Ensures conclusions are based on authentic data. | **Cellebrite**, **Oxygen**, **Autopsy** (for file integrity). |\n| **4.5 Hypothesis Generation & Testing** | \u2022 Formulate hypotheses (e.g., suspect was at Scene A from 10:00\u201310:15).<br>\u2022 Test against all data sources. | Provides a structured narrative for the report. | None (analytical). |\n| **4.6 Documentation of Findings** | \u2022 Record all steps, tools, settings, and results.<br>\u2022 Capture screenshots, export tables. | Required for reproducibility and court admissibility. | **Microsoft Word**, **Adobe PDF**, **Excel**. |\n\n---\n\n## 5. Legal & Ethical Considerations\n\n| Issue | Mitigation |\n|-------|------------|\n| **Privacy** | Only collect data directly relevant to the investigation.
